	    int option = 0;  // Declare option variable outside the try block

	    try {
	        option = (int) getUserInput1();  // Get and store user input

	        switch (option) {
	            case 1:
	                printMenu();
	                clearscreen();
	                break;
	            case 2:
	                aboutUs();
	                break;
	            case 3:
	                exitScreen();
	                break;
	            default:
	                error();  // Handle invalid options
	                break;
	        }


	    } catch (Exception e) {
	        clearscreen();
	       error();
	        e.printStackTrace();
	        error();  // Optional: show generic error message
	    }
	}

		    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
		    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
		    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
		    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
		    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
		    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
		    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
		    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
		    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");

		    try {
		     	int option;
		         option = getUserInput1();  // Method returns validated integer input

		         switch (option) {
		             case 1:
		                 calculator();
		                break;
		             case 2:
		                 conversionMenu();
		                 break;
		             case 3:
		            	 clearscreen();
		                 areaCircumferenceCircle();
		                 break;
		             case 4:
		                 startscreen();
		                 break;
		             case 5:
		            	 exitScreen();
		             default:
		                 error();  // Handle any number not 1-4
		                 break;
		         }
		    } catch (Exception e) {
		        clearscreen();
		       error();
		        e.printStackTrace();
		        error();  // Optional: show generic error message
		    }
		}



	static void calculator() {
		clearscreen();
		Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+PURPLE + "_________     _____  .____   _________  ____ ___.____       ________________________ __________                                                                                                    \r\n"
	    		+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ "\\_   ___ \\   /  _  \\ |    |  \\_   ___ \\|    |   \\    |     /  _  \\__    ___/\\_____  \\\\______   \\                                                                                                   \r\n"
	    		+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ "\\     \\____/    |    \\    |__\\     \\___|    |  /|    |___/    |    \\    |   /    |    \\    |   \\                                                                                                    \r\n"
	    		+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ " \\______  /\\____|__  /_______ \\______  /______/ |_______ \\____|__  /____|   \\_______  /____|_  /                                                                                                    \r\n"
	    		+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ "        \\/         \\/        \\/      \\/                 \\/       \\/                 \\/       \\/                                                                                                  "+RESET);
	  
	    System.out.print("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"Enter first number: ");
	    double a = Double.parseDouble(sc.nextLine());
	    System.out.print("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"Enter operator (+, -, *, /): ");    
	    char op = sc.nextLine().charAt(0);
	    System.out.print("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"Enter second number: ");
	 
	    double b = Double.parseDouble(sc.nextLine());
	    double result = 0;
	    switch (op) {
	        case '+': result = a + b; break;
	        case '-': result = a - b; break;
	        case '*': result = a * b; break;
	        case '/': result = (b != 0) ? a / b : Double.NaN; break;
	        default:
	           error();
	            return;
	    }
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"║"+ YELLOW + "     Result: " + result + RESET+"                                          ║║"+GREEN+"                   (1) Back ↩                                        (2) Exit 🏠︎  "+RESET+"                                                  ║    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
		System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"║                                                          ║║                		                                                                                                         ║    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");

	    
	    try {

	    	 String input = sc.nextLine(); // Always read as string first
	    	 int number = Integer.parseInt(input);
	     	int option;
	         option = getUserInput1();  // Method returns validated integer input

	    switch (option) {
	        case 1:
	            startscreen();
	            clearscreen();
	            break;
	        case 2:
	        	exitScreen();
	            break;
	        
	        default:
	            error(); 
	            break;
	    }

	    } catch (Exception e) {
	        clearscreen();
	       error();
	        e.printStackTrace();
	        error();  // Optional: show generic error message
	    }
	}

	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");

	}


	static void unitConversion() {
		clearscreen();
		Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
		System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+PURPLE + " ____ __________  .______________ _________  ________    ___________   _________________________  _________.___________    _______                                                                                                      \r\n"
				+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ "|    |   \\      \\ |   \\__    ___/ \\_   ___ \\ \\_____  \\   \\      \\   \\ /   /\\_   _____/\\______   \\/   _____/|   \\_____  \\   \\      \\                                                                                                     \r\n"
				+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ "|    |   /   |   \\|   | |    |    /    \\  \\/  /   |   \\  /   |   \\   Y   /  |    __)_  |       _/\\_____  \\ |   |/   |   \\  /   |   \\                                                                                                    \r\n"
				+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ "|    |  /    |    \\   | |    |    \\     \\____/    |    \\/    |    \\     /   |        \\ |    |   \\/        \\|   /    |    \\/    |    \\                                                                                                   \r\n"
				+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ "|______/\\____|__  /___| |____|     \\______  /\\_______  /\\____|__  /\\___/   /_______  / |____|_  /_______  /|___\\_______  /\\____|__  /                                                                                                   \r\n"
				+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ "                \\/                        \\/         \\/         \\/                 \\/         \\/        \\/             \\/         \\/                                                                                                    "+RESET);
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+GREEN + "Enter value and unit (mm/cm/m):" + RESET);
	    System.out.print("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t" +"Value: ");
	    double value = Double.parseDouble(sc.nextLine());
	    System.out.print("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"Unit (mm/cm/m): ");
	    String unit = sc.nextLine().toLowerCase();
	    double mm, cm, m;
	    switch (unit) {
	        case "mm":
	            mm = value;
	            cm = value / 10;
	            m = value / 1000;
	            break;
	        case "cm":
	            mm = value * 10;
	            cm = value;
	            m = value / 100;
	            break;
	        case "m":
	            mm = value * 1000;
	            cm = value * 100;
	            m = value;
	            break;
	        default:
	            error();
	return;
	    }
	    System.out.printf("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+YELLOW + "%.2f mm = %.2f cm = %.2f m\n" + RESET, mm, cm, m);
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                      ╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"                              ║"+GREEN+"                   (1) Back ↩                                        (2) Exit 🏠︎  "+RESET+"                                                  ║    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
		System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"                              ║                		                                                                                                           ║    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"                              ╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");

	    
	    try {
	     	int option;
	         option = getUserInput1();  // Method returns validated integer input

	    switch (option) {
	        case 1:
	            startscreen();
	            clearscreen();
	            break;
	        case 2:
	            exitScreen();
	            break;
	        
	        default:
	            error();  // Handle any number not 1-4
	            break;
	    }

	    } catch (NumberFormatException e) { // Catch the specific error for conversion failure
		    error();
		    // ... or display your custom error screen/message ...
		} catch (Exception e) { // Catch any other unexpected errors
		    error();
		    
		}
	}

	static void oddEvenConversion() {
		clearscreen();
		Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
		System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+PURPLE + "________  ________  ________      ____    _______________   _______________ _______                                                                                                     \r\n"
				+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ "\\_____  \\ \\______ \\ \\______ \\    /  _ \\   \\_   _____/\\   \\ /   /\\_   _____/ \\      \\                                                                                                    \r\n"
				+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ " /   |   \\ |    |  \\ |    |  \\   >  _ </\\  |    __)_  \\   Y   /  |    __)_  /   |   \\                                                                                                   \r\n"
				+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ "/    |    \\|    `   \\|    `   \\ /  <_\\ \\/  |        \\  \\     /   |        \\/    |    \\                                                                                                  \r\n"
				+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ "\\_______  /_______  /_______  / \\_____\\ \\ /_______  /   \\___/   /_______  /\\____|__  /                                                                                                  \r\n"
				+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+ "        \\/        \\/        \\/         \\/         \\/                    \\/         \\/                                                                                                   "+RESET);
	    System.out.print("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"Enter a number: ");
	    
	    try {

	    int num = Integer.parseInt(sc.nextLine());
	    String result = (num % 2 == 0) ? "Even" : "Odd";
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"║"+YELLOW + "The number " + num + " is " + result + "." + RESET+"                                    ║║"+GREEN+"               (1) Back ↩                                        (2) Exit 🏠︎  "+RESET+"                                                      ║    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
		System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"║                                                          ║║                		                                                                                                         ║    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    
	    } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
	    	error();
	    	
	    
	    }
	    try {
	     	int option;
	         option = getUserInput1();  // Method returns validated integer input

	    switch (option) {
	        case 1:
	            startscreen();
	            clearscreen();
	            break;
	        case 2:
	            exitScreen();
	            break;
	        
	        default:
	            error();  // Handle any number not 1-4
	            break;
	    }

	} catch (InterruptedException e) {
	  error();
	    Thread.currentThread().interrupt();  // Restore interrupted state
	}
	}

	static void areaCircumferenceCircle() {
		Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
	    System.out.println(PURPLE+"\t\t\t\t\t" + "           _____                           ____    _________ .__                              _____                                                  _____           _________ .__               .__                                                            \r\n"
	    		+"\t\t\t\t\t"+ "  /  _  \\_______   ____ _____     /  _ \\   \\_   ___ \\|__|______   ____  __ __  ______/ ____\\___________   ____   ____   ____  ____     _____/ ____\\ _____    \\_   ___ \\|__|______   ____ |  |   ____                                                    \r\n"
	    		+"\t\t\t\t\t"+ " /  /_\\  \\_  __ \\_/ __ \\\\__  \\    >  _ </\\ /    \\  \\/|  \\_  __ \\_/ ___\\|  |  \\/     \\   __\\/ __ \\_  __ \\_/ __ \\ /    \\_/ ___\\/ __ \\   /  _ \\   __\\  \\__  \\   /    \\  \\/|  \\_  __ \\_/ ___\\|  | _/ __ \\                                                   \r\n"
	    		+"\t\t\t\t\t"+ "/    |    \\  | \\/\\  ___/ / __ \\_ /  <_\\ \\/ \\     \\___|  ||  | \\/\\  \\___|  |  /  Y Y  \\  | \\  ___/|  | \\/\\  ___/|   |  \\  \\__\\  ___/  (  <_> )  |     / __ \\_ \\     \\___|  ||  | \\/\\  \\___|  |_\\  ___/                                                   \r\n"
	    		+"\t\t\t\t\t"+ "\\____|__  /__|    \\___  >____  / \\_____\\ \\  \\______  /__||__|    \\___  >____/|__|_|  /__|  \\___  >__|    \\___  >___|  /\\___  >___  >  \\____/|__|    (____  /  \\______  /__||__|    \\___  >____/\\___  >                                                  \r\n"
	    		+"\t\t\t\t\t"+ "        \\/            \\/     \\/         \\/         \\/                \\/            \\/          \\/            \\/     \\/     \\/    \\/                      \\/          \\/                \\/          \\/                                                   " + RESET);
	    System.out.print("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"Enter radius: ");
	    try {
	    double r = Double.parseDouble(sc.nextLine());
	    double area = Math.PI * r * r;
	    double circumference = 2 * Math.PI * r;
	    System.out.printf("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+YELLOW + "Area: %.2f\n"+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"Circumference: %.2f\n" + RESET, area, circumference);
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t"+"                                                                                                               "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"                              ╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"                              ║"+GREEN+"                   (1) Back ↩                                        (2) Exit 🏠︎  "+RESET+"                                                  ║    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
		System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"                              ║                		                                                                                                           ║    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");
	    System.out.println("\t\t\t\t\t"+"                              ╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝    "+"\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t");

	    	
	 	     	int option;
	 	         option = getUserInput1();  // Method returns validated integer input
	  
	         switch (option) {
	             case 1:
	                 startscreen();
	                 clearscreen();
	                 break;
	             case 2:
	                 exitScreen();
	                 break;
	             
	             default:
	                 error();  // Handle any number not 1-4
	                 break;
	         }

	     } catch (InterruptedException e) {
	         error();
	         Thread.currentThread().interrupt();  // Restore interrupted state
	         
		    }
		    try {
		     	int option;
		         option = getUserInput1();  // Method returns validated integer input
	 
	        switch (option) {
	            case 1:
	                startscreen();
	                clearscreen();
	                break;
	            case 2:
	                exitScreen();
	                break;
	            
	            default:
	                error();  // Handle any number not 1-4
	                break;
	        }

	    } catch (InterruptedException e) {
	       error();
	        Thread.currentThread().interrupt();  // Restore interrupted state
	    
	    }
	}

	    }
	}

	static void exitScreen() {

		    int option;

		    try {
		        option = getUserInput1();  // Get and store user input

		        switch (option) {
		            case 1:
		                clearscreen();
		                startscreen();
		                break;
		            case 2:
		            	clearscreen();
		                exitScreen();
		                break;
		            default:
		                error();  // Invalid option
		                break;
		        }
		    } catch (Exception e) {
		        clearscreen();
		        e.printStackTrace();
		        error();  // Optional: show generic error message
		    }
		}




	public static int getUserInput1() throws InterruptedException {
	    Scanner input = new Scanner(System.in);
	    int value = 0;
	    boolean validInput = false;

	    while (!validInput) {
	        System.out.print("Enter a number: ");
	        String userInput = input.nextLine();  // Read the entire line as a string

	        if (userInput.isEmpty()) {  // Check if the input is empty
	            error();
	            continue;  // Skip the rest of the loop and prompt again
	        }

	        try {
	            value = Integer.parseInt(userInput);  // Try to parse the input as a number
	            validInput = true;  // If successful, mark it as valid input
	        } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
	            error();  // Handle non-integer input
	        }
	    }

	    return value;
	}

	}
